\"source/server/admin/prometheus_stats.cc\"\n    }\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Envoy stats system is organized into several key components implemented across the v1.31.2 codebase:\\n\\n## Core Stats Hierarchy (envoy/stats/)\\n\\nThe foundational interfaces are defined in envoy/stats/. The Stats::Scope hierarchy is defined in scope.h, representing scoped statistics that inherit from parent scopes. The Store interface (store.h) manages all scopes and provides access to the root scope. The Allocator interface (allocator.h) is responsible for creating new stat metrics.\\n\\n## Stat Name Interning (StatNamePool)\\n\\nStatistic names are interned through the SymbolTable mechanism (source/common/stats/symbol_table.h and symbol_table.cc). The StatNamePool class provides pooled allocation and management of StatName objects for efficient memory reuse. This is a critical optimization for handling high-cardinality metric names without excessive memory consumption.\\n\\n## Tag Extraction Architecture\\n\\nTags are extracted from metric names through a two-level system:\\n- TagExtractor interface and implementations (envoy/stats/tag_extractor.h, source/common/stats/tag_extractor_impl.h/cc): Provides regex-based and fixed-value tag extraction patterns\\n- TagProducer interface and implementation (envoy/stats/tag_producer.h, source/common/stats/tag_producer_impl.h/cc): Coordinates multiple extractors to extract all tags from a metric name\\n- TagUtility (source/common/stats/tag_utility.h/cc): Helper functions for tag operations and StatName construction with tags\\n\\n## Thread-Local Store Implementation\\n\\nThe thread-safe, high-performance stats store is implemented in source/common/stats/thread_local_store.h/cc. The ThreadLocalStoreImpl::ScopeImpl class manages per-scope metrics and provides methods like counterFromStatNameWithTags, gaugeFromStatNameWithTags, and histogramFromStatNameWithTags. The implementation includes thread-local caching and proper scope hierarchy management.\\n\\n## Alternative Store Implementations\\n\\nThe IsolatedStoreImpl (source/common/stats/isolated_store_impl.h/cc) provides a non-thread-safe implementation useful for testing and isolated stat collections. Both implementations support the common Store interface for polymorphism.\\n\\n## Metric Implementation\\n\\nIndividual metric types are implemented in:\\n- histogram_impl.h/cc: Counter, gauge, and histogram metric implementations including thread-local histograms (ThreadLocalHistogramImpl) and parent histograms (ParentHistogramImpl)\\n- metric_impl.h/cc: Base MetricHelper class providing common metric functionality\\n- Null implementations (null_counter.h, null_gauge.h, null_text_readout.h): No-op metrics for disabled stats\\n\\n## Sink Architecture and Dispatch\\n\\nThe Sink interface (envoy/stats/sink.h) defines how stats are flushed to external systems. The dispatch mechanism is implemented in the Store, which maintains a list of sinks and calls onStaticCountersIterator, onHistogramComplete, etc. on each sink.\\n\\n## Stat Sink Implementations\\n\\nMultiple sink implementations handle different output formats:\\n\\n1. **StatsD/Metrics Service (source/extensions/stat_sinks/common/statsd/)**: \\n   - UdpStatsdSink and TcpStatsdSink implement statsd protocol output\\n   - tag_formats.h/cc handles different tagging conventions (Datadog, InfluxDB, etc.)\\n\\n2. **Statsd Factory (source/extensions/stat_sinks/statsd/)**: config.h/cc registers the statsd sink factory\\n\\n3. **DogStatsd (source/extensions/stat_sinks/dog_statsd/)**: Datadog-compatible statsd sink factory\\n\\n4. **GraphiteStatsd (source/extensions/stat_sinks/graphite_statsd/)**: Graphite-compatible statsd sink factory\\n\\n5. **Hystrix (source/extensions/stat_sinks/hystrix/)**: \\n   - hystrix.h/cc implements the Hystrix dashboard compatible sink\\n   - Provides real-time metrics for Hystrix circuit breaker visualization\\n\\n6. **gRPC Metrics Service (source/extensions/stat_sinks/metrics_service/)**: \\n   - grpc_metrics_service_impl.h/cc implements templated MetricsServiceSink\\n   - Supports flushing to external metrics services via gRPC\\n   - grpc_metrics_proto_descriptors.h/cc provides proto definitions\\n\\n7. **OpenTelemetry (source/extensions/stat_sinks/open_telemetry/)**: \\n   - open_telemetry_impl.h/cc provides OpenTelemetry-compatible metrics export\\n   - Supports OTLP protocol for modern observability platforms\\n\\n8. **Wasm (source/extensions/stat_sinks/wasm/)**: \\n   - wasm_stat_sink_impl.h enables stats sinks written in WebAssembly\\n   - Allows extensible sink implementations without core changes\\n\\n## Prometheus Output\\n\\nThe Prometheus stats formatter (source/server/admin/prometheus_stats.h/cc) converts Envoy stats to Prometheus text format for the /stats/prometheus admin endpoint. This uses the tag extraction system to properly format Prometheus labels.\\n\\n## Supporting Systems\\n\\n- **StatsMatcherImpl (stats_matcher_impl.h/cc)**: Implements stat filtering based on inclusion/exclusion patterns\\n- **Allocator Implementation (allocator_impl.h/cc)**: Manages memory allocation and lifecycle for metric objects\\n- **StatMerger (stat_merger.h/cc)**: Merges stats from multiple Envoy processes (used in hot restart)\\n- **Deferred Creation (deferred_creation.h)**: Supports lazy initialization of stats structures\\n\\nThe architecture ensures lock-free fast-path access on per-thread caches while maintaining global stat consistency through proper synchronization on the slow path.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":254,"cache_read_input_tokens":89812,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":254},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"ab6132cc-7739-4df2-8a66-08548b15e297","uuid":"816b2f71-e8f6-410f-983c-34f97ecb388b"}

The Allocator interface (allocator.h) is responsible for creating new stat metrics.\\n\\n## Stat Name Interning (StatNamePool)\\n\\nStatistic names are interned through the SymbolTable mechanism (source/common/stats/symbol_table.h and symbol_table.cc). The StatNamePool class provides pooled allocation and management of StatName objects for efficient memory reuse. This is a critical optimization for handling high-cardinality metric names without excessive memory consumption.\\n\\n## Tag Extraction Architecture\\n\\nTags are extracted from metric names through a two-level system:\\n- TagExtractor interface and implementations (envoy/stats/tag_extractor.h, source/common/stats/tag_extractor_impl.h/cc): Provides regex-based and fixed-value tag extraction patterns\\n- TagProducer interface and implementation (envoy/stats/tag_producer.h, source/common/stats/tag_producer_impl.h/cc): Coordinates multiple extractors to extract all tags from a metric name\\n- TagUtility (source/common/stats/tag_utility.h/cc): Helper functions for tag operations and StatName construction with tags\\n\\n## Thread-Local Store Implementation\\n\\nThe thread-safe, high-performance stats store is implemented in source/common/stats/thread_local_store.h/cc. The ThreadLocalStoreImpl::ScopeImpl class manages per-scope metrics and provides methods like counterFromStatNameWithTags, gaugeFromStatNameWithTags, and histogramFromStatNameWithTags. The implementation includes thread-local caching and proper scope hierarchy management.\\n\\n## Alternative Store Implementations\\n\\nThe IsolatedStoreImpl (source/common/stats/isolated_store_impl.h/cc) provides a non-thread-safe implementation useful for testing and isolated stat collections. Both implementations support the common Store interface for polymorphism.\\n\\n## Metric Implementation\\n\\nIndividual metric types are implemented in:\\n- histogram_impl.h/cc: Counter, gauge, and histogram metric implementations including thread-local histograms (ThreadLocalHistogramImpl) and parent histograms (ParentHistogramImpl)\\n- metric_impl.h/cc: Base MetricHelper class providing common metric functionality\\n- Null implementations (null_counter.h, null_gauge.h, null_text_readout.h): No-op metrics for disabled stats\\n\\n## Sink Architecture and Dispatch\\n\\nThe Sink interface (envoy/stats/sink.h) defines how stats are flushed to external systems. The dispatch mechanism is implemented in the Store, which maintains a list of sinks and calls onStaticCountersIterator, onHistogramComplete, etc. on each sink.\\n\\n## Stat Sink Implementations\\n\\nMultiple sink implementations handle different output formats:\\n\\n1. **StatsD/Metrics Service (source/extensions/stat_sinks/common/statsd/)**: \\n   - UdpStatsdSink and TcpStatsdSink implement statsd protocol output\\n   - tag_formats.h/cc handles different tagging conventions (Datadog, InfluxDB, etc.)\\n\\n2. **Statsd Factory (source/extensions/stat_sinks/statsd/)**: config.h/cc registers the statsd sink factory\\n\\n3. **DogStatsd (source/extensions/stat_sinks/dog_statsd/)**: Datadog-compatible statsd sink factory\\n\\n4. **GraphiteStatsd (source/extensions/stat_sinks/graphite_statsd/)**: Graphite-compatible statsd sink factory\\n\\n5. **Hystrix (source/extensions/stat_sinks/hystrix/)**: \\n   - hystrix.h/cc implements the Hystrix dashboard compatible sink\\n   - Provides real-time metrics for Hystrix circuit breaker visualization\\n\\n6. **gRPC Metrics Service (source/extensions/stat_sinks/metrics_service/)**: \\n   - grpc_metrics_service_impl.h/cc implements templated MetricsServiceSink\\n   - Supports flushing to external metrics services via gRPC\\n   - grpc_metrics_proto_descriptors.h/cc provides proto definitions\\n\\n7. **OpenTelemetry (source/extensions/stat_sinks/open_telemetry/)**: \\n   - open_telemetry_impl.h/cc provides OpenTelemetry-compatible metrics export\\n   - Supports OTLP protocol for modern observability platforms\\n\\n8. **Wasm (source/extensions/stat_sinks/wasm/)**: \\n   - wasm_stat_sink_impl.h enables stats sinks written in WebAssembly\\n   - Allows extensible sink implementations without core changes\\n\\n## Prometheus Output\\n\\nThe Prometheus stats formatter (source/server/admin/prometheus_stats.h/cc) converts Envoy stats to Prometheus text format for the /stats/prometheus admin endpoint. This uses the tag extraction system to properly format Prometheus labels.\\n\\n## Supporting Systems\\n\\n- **StatsMatcherImpl (stats_matcher_impl.h/cc)**: Implements stat filtering based on inclusion/exclusion patterns\\n- **Allocator Implementation (allocator_impl.h/cc)**: Manages memory allocation and lifecycle for metric objects\\n- **StatMerger (stat_merger.h/cc)**: Merges stats from multiple Envoy processes (used in hot restart)\\n- **Deferred Creation (deferred_creation.h)**: Supports lazy initialization of stats structures\\n\\nThe architecture ensures lock-free fast-path access on per-thread caches while maintaining global stat consistency through proper synchronization on the slow path.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
